< Text>
Great customer service first of all. They even stopped by our table to check on us to see if everything was ok. You don't see this at all at fast food places.

Food was fantastic. True Mexican taste. I would definitely come here again. The tables were a bit sticky, but we cleaned it up pretty good. Limited seating for such a busy place.

Again, great tasting authentic mexican food in a fast food environment. Check out my channel Simply Tom to see my eating videos here. It's pretty darn good. Food, that is. lol.< /Text>

< text>
The fish tacos are plentiful, crunchy and well garnished, very good choice if a Taco Nazo isn't nearby. The included salsa is flavorful with mild heat. Taco Tuesdays make for a reasonably priced weekly meal. Beer would be a much welcomed addition to compliment the menu. Dining area is small and clean. The garnish station is adequate, I like more variety. Despite the off-road racing decor, the TV is tuned to novellas, variety shows and soccer. The staff is nice and orders are filled quickly. Drive thru got my order wrong the only time I've used it, at least they were shrimp tacos; tasted good, but I'm glad I wasn't allergic.</text>

October 2018 I asked to exchanged for another one due to their product was defective, they will try to blame you first or your mechanics, make up some excuses to avoid return or exchange. To make long story short they agreed but I was told that it will be more expensive because its a better quality.

< Text>
Tightly packed, micro store with a lot of uncommon vinyl in really good condition. Friendly and knowledgable staff. The store is very small though and only a couple people can fit in there at a time so you may need to take turns getting in and out. Lots of great finds in there and it is really worth the stop if you are in the neighborhood. They have a little of everything, including some great local bands. The prices were good and the vinyl was well worth the purchase price. Cool place with an old school feel. One of the best hole in the wall shops I have been to.</Text>

It's a small place (>200 sqft), but packed with records. They are reasonably well organized for the type of place, but you still have to dig a bit. The prices vary from $~4 for poor quality to $~20 for good and on up.

<review>My wife Kendall and I took our cat here to be checked out. She keeps scratching her ear and we don't know why (and still don't know why). Pleasanton Veterinary Hospital, without actually seeing our cat prescribed a variety of medications and put her on a diet trial for 3 months and insisted she be in a cone for that duration of time. When asked to bring our cat in, they refused to examine our cat, claiming she was swiping at them, even though they also said they never took her out of the cat carrier to begin with (there was no way she could have gotten her paw through the holes in the cat carrier). They prescribed Gabapentin, an anticonvulsant medication claiming this would stop her from swiping at them in future visits and were gracious enough to charge us for it. Our cat was calm and fine going to and from the vet and is by nature and extremely friendly cat who sits in peoples laps when she meets them and we have never had this kind of issue with any other vet. We gave our cat this medication as prescribed, as well as daily dosages of Prednisolone (a steroid) and an anxiety medication and brought her back to the vet. They said she was still swiping at them (still having never taken her out of the cat carrier) and refused to examine our cat, told us to keep our cat in a cone and keep her on a diet trial for another 3 months while charging us for these visits and still having not examined or cat to see if this is even warranted. They graciously charged us for an examination both times without examining our cat and without providing any possible solutions other than long term medication, change of diet and continuous wearing of a cone. When told we would be soliciting a second opinion, they were very quick to give us our cat back without any pleasantries. I do not recommend this vet.<//review>< Pics>

< review>
I went to a 24 hour veterinary hospital in Dublin, CA, for a year. I left when my "Rosita" was taken from me by a heartless, nonchalant, rude, non empathetic human being.
I thought I would never own another dog. Rosita's death shattered most of my heart. She was my "Emotional Support Therapy" dog and she loved me as much as I loved her.
After a few months of crying, sleeping and isolation, I decided to look online at the animal shelter in Dublin.
I was scanning pictures of the potential adoptees and my finger stopped. There she was, this cute, little imp of a face, with ears laid back. That was it!! She was staring back at me, with tiny, black eyes, yearning for her "forever" home.
I immediately called the shelter and asked if this sweet precious was still available for adoption. She was!!!
I jumped out of bed, got dressed and was there, faster than "greased lightening"!!
I was waiting in the yard, and one of the attendants opened the door. There she was, running on her leash like a banshee.
I picked her up and she curled up in my lap. I was a goner for this sweet girl. Turned out, she's a "Senior", just like me, with two, rather large, bald spots and a few, rotten teeth.
She received a vet check and I was told she is a "Chinese Crested" and ??? else.
It really was "love at first sight"!!!
I was on the hunt for a new doctor for "Miss Molly". We both decided that "Pleasanton Veterinary Hospital" would be our medical, grooming, nutritional facility.
The administrative employees, vet techs and veterinarians are ALL caring, knowledgeable, empathetic and kind. We've ALWAYS been treated like family and Miss Molly is always calm and collected, when we are there.
We are both very happy to recommend "Pleasanton Veterinary Hospital" for your animals' medical, grooming and nutritional needs.</review>

< Review>
If only all businesses had such nice people! Here it is affordable and the service is very caring. I was so frustrated with other vets I dealt with in South San Jose and Palo Alto. The other vets had no empathy and they wanted to charge an arm and a leg, pushing for same day surgery of the wrong limb, and not answering my questions stating that they will answer it next time or the next specialist will answer the questions. With the care I've had so far here, I do not regret the 1 hr drive. Pleasanton Veterinary Hospital has called back to answer questions and followup on concerns regarding the surgery. I will recommend this vet hospital 100% to anyone I know. So far so very worth it!!!<//Review>

< Review>
Yesterday I went for the first time to Dublin's. I never felt like going before because some people had told me bad things about it. I wanted to give it a try though. The only thing I got was bad service. Both clerks were drunk, you could clearly smell it in their breath and in the way they were serving costumers. I wanted to go to the bathroom before ordering, and in my way there I was approached by a guy I honestly thought wanted to pick up a fight, but no.. I later learned he was one of the bartenders. He grabbed me by the arm and pushed me out of the bathroom hallway asking for my id. I understand that bars can get a big fine for not checking IDs, but that's not the way of handling the situation. I pulled out my ID while I was being dragged out of the bar, and told him that he was not practicing good customer service. He just smiled and laughed at everything I was saying. I realized he was drunk and there was no point in reasoning with him, so I took my friends and left. On the way out, people were asking why we were leaving and started complaining too. I'm not going back to this bar again.<//Review>

< text>
Good value overall. There are only two coin op car washes in Tustin/North Irvine area: these guys and the guys down the road. This one is cleaner, have better amenity, has a dog wash station, and got bigger lot but at more cost compared to the other one. This place is always lit well 24/7, there is less need to worry about being robbed or something. My complaint is that when used credit card, the $5/10min option is chosen automatically with no way of changing at all. Bring cash if you want their regular option. There is a blower-dryer option, but I don't feel like it's a very good one and you're probably better off just using your own towels to wipe the car. I'd still pick this car wash over any gas station car washes which are just plain rip offs at least the ones I saw in Irvine.<//text>

This is my fourth Smog Certificate from John.  He is competitively priced, considerate and thorough.  They keep things strictly legal, while doing their best to guide a customer through to legitimately passing a Smog test.
